Lawyers Owing Membership Dues Take Note: Once Reported, They Cannot Appear in Court 134

The Shanghai Lawyers Association has over nine hundred members. The regular membership dues of the association, as approved by the Ministry of Judicial Administration in the association's charter, stipulate that if a member owes membership dues for more than four months, the association can report the delinquent member for withdrawal from the association. Recently, the association found that there were as many as twenty-nine members who had owed regular membership dues for more than ten months. Therefore, it was brought up for discussion at the 125th joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees, and it was resolved to report these twenty-nine members to courts at all levels for withdrawal from the association. However, after being reported, these lawyers will not be able to appear in court. Therefore, for convenience, the association will leave the reporting documents unsealed at the association for three days and will notify each member who owes dues again, requiring them to pay the full amount of regular membership dues owed within these three days. If they fail to pay within the deadline, the documents will be sent out as required.

Lake Society Issues Bonds 135

The bond amount is 15,000 yuan in national currency. Pan Gongzhan and others are members of the bond committee. The Lake Society on Guizhou Road in this city reported to the National Government last year and was approved to build a memorial hall for the martyr Chen Ying Shi in the society's premises. It has now been fully completed this summer. The construction funds were raised over several years, collecting huge sums. A portion of the donations were in the form of public bonds, which could not be used as cash. Loans were repeatedly borrowed from banks, but they were still insufficient. It is estimated that the project funds and the cost of purchasing internal equipment and appliances will still require about 10,000 taels of silver. The tenth executive committee meeting of the society resolved to issue bonds worth 15,000 yuan in national currency to meet urgent needs and organized a bond committee, appointing Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yiting, Chen Aishi, Qian Xinzhi, Shen Tianxin, and others as members responsible for handling the matter. It was also decided to start issuing them on New Year's Day next year.

Wu Mituo Sues for Inheritance 138

Since the promulgation of the Inheritance Section of the Civil Code, there have been countless cases of women petitioning the court to inherit their father's estate. After the National Government announced that women's claims to inherit property would only be valid if their father's death occurred after the National Government's power reached the area, and after the Judicial Yuan issued a unified interpretation of the law abolishing the right of representation, the number of lawsuits over inheritance disputes has decreased significantly. Recently, the First Special Court accepted a case in which Wu Mituo, a local woman, sued her brother, Wu Changsheng, demanding payment of inheritance. The woman's father, Miao Fu, died in 1925. At that time, Jiangsu Province was still under the jurisdiction of Sun Chuanfang, and the power of the National Government had not yet reached the area. According to the law, she had no right to inherit. However, the woman claimed that she was her father's favorite and that she was 36 years old and had not yet married. A precedent set by the former Supreme Court in its third year, case number 669, stated that if a daughter was favored by her father, she could request a reasonable share of the inheritance. Therefore, Wu hired Feng Xizui and Wu Zhengzhao, two lawyers, to sue Wu Changsheng in the First Special Court, demanding a reasonable share of 100,000 yuan from her late father's estate of 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. Her lawsuit listed how her stepmother, Sheng, and the defendant had abused her, stating that the defendant sat on an estate of 400,000 to 500,000 yuan, living in luxury, while the plaintiff had to work as a servant. The situations of the two parties were as different as heaven and earth. Yesterday, Judge Ding Dehan of the First Special Court opened the Fifth Civil Division for questioning. The defendant, Wu Changsheng, hired Zhang Zhengxue and Fang Jiahe, two lawyers, to defend him. According to Wu Mituo's testimony, after my father died, the defendant and others beat me and refused to let me in. Now I am working as a servant in the home of a certain family on Beijing Road. My father loved me very much when he was alive and was very strict in choosing a marriage partner for me, so I have not yet married. Now I am asking the defendant to give me a reasonable share of 100,000 yuan from the inheritance. When questioned, Wu Changsheng testified that the plaintiff did not abide by family rules when her father was alive and had an affair with Zhang Fulin from Shuanglin, cohabiting at Number 7, Minren Lane, Mintini Yin Road. The plaintiff ran away on her own in 1926, taking valuable jewelry with her. Furthermore, my late father's estate consists only of a few bungalows and a cemetery, with a total value of no more than 10,000 yuan. Moreover, all of them cannot be sold. What the plaintiff said is an exaggeration. If the court does not believe me, it can investigate. He also presented maternal uncles Zhang Xinting and Zhang Youting, uncles Wu Xinqing and Wu Xingen, and stepmother Wu Sheng as witnesses to prove that the plaintiff did indeed run away with the jewelry. The court briefly questioned each witness and then began the debate. After the two lawyers debated, the judge reserved the verdict for a scheduled pronouncement.

County Border Intellectual Bandit Suspects Sent to Court 139

Clear Interrogation and Transfer for Trial

Recently, in various towns and villages such as Tangwan and Caohang in the second district of the county, major cases of robbery, kidnapping, and extortion have occurred one after another. After investigation by the county government, it was found that these cases were all committed by a group of local idle intellectuals. The Public Security Section was immediately ordered to supervise the detectives to arrest Peng Jieren, Chen Zhuxin, Chen Haiqing, Zhang Zhaoxiang, Sun Linsheng, and suspects Liu Junfu, Chen Haishan, and Wang A'tudi, a total of eight people, in the district and the British and French concessions. Now, under the order of County Magistrate Yan, Peng and the other eight criminals were transferred to the local court yesterday with a written record for trial.

Social Evils 140

Gun Bullets in Peanuts. The Municipal Public Security Bureau Detective Team recently received a tip that a batch of firearms was hidden in a dried goods shop at Number 305, Wangjia Wharf, Nanshi, and was planning to be secretly transported to other ports. The team dispatched personnel to the address on the previous day, accompanied by Mao Jiming, a police officer from the first precinct of the first district, to search the store carefully. After a long time, they found 1,200 rifle bullets hidden in a bag of peanuts. The store owner, Fu Bingfang, Zhu Zhike, and Shen Yuming, all from Shandong, along with the seized evidence, were taken to the first precinct of the first district. During the preliminary hearing by the police chief, Fu Bingfang and others confessed to intending to transport and sell the firearms to other ports. They were then taken back to the bureau for further investigation.

Reiterating the Prohibition of Pulling Bristles. Every time pig boats arrive at Youche Wharf in Nanshi, some people forcibly pull bristles from live pigs. This act has long been strictly prohibited by the authorities. However, recently, after a long time, the problem has resurfaced. Director Wen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, considering that these people are disregarding the ban and acting extremely unlawfully, specially notified the first precinct of the first district to instruct all relevant police officers to take note. In the future, if anyone is found forcibly pulling pig bristles, they should be taken to the bureau for strict punishment.

Conference Staff: Presidium: Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Shi Liangcai, Lin Kanghou; Recorder: Shao Xubai; Master of Ceremonies: Cao Zhigong; Reception: Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xianggao, Li Mengnan, Li Yongxiang, Liu Xinquan, Liu Yiwen, Tang Daxin, Yang Jiaoqi.

Ceremony: At 3:00 PM, the opening ceremony was held in the Freedom Hall. First, the music team of the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School played music. Then, the presidium took their seats, sang the Party song, and the military band of the Public Security Bureau played the score. The Party and National Flags and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen were given the highest respect. Sun Yat-sen's will was read aloud. Then, Chairman Yu Qiaqing reported on the event, followed by Ren Jinping reporting on the preparations. Next, guests Lu Jingshi, Lin Kanghou, and Tao Leqin, and variety show director Zhang Baichuan gave speeches. Finally, Deputy Executive Director Zhu Xuefan gave a reply. After the Postal Workers' Orchestra played music, photos were taken, and the ceremony was declared over.

Chairman's Speech: Chairman Yu Qiaqing's opening speech briefly stated that the refugees in northern Jiangsu are under the iron heel of the violent Japanese, in the midst of ice and snow. With great righteousness, they pledge their courage and use their hot blood and heads to fight the strong enemy. They sleep in the open air, endure hunger and cold. Their hard work and unwavering spirit are worthy of lasting admiration. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other four groups have specially launched a variety show to raise huge sums of money for relief and plan to use the variety show to promote awareness, hoping to awaken compatriots' attention and jointly provide practical assistance. Report on the Process: Staff member Ren Jinping reported on the preparations, saying that this variety show was initiated by the four groups and that preparations were rushed, so there were many imperfections, for which he expressed deep apologies. It is painful to use variety shows for national salvation. However, he hopes to use the power of variety shows to publicize the suffering of refugees, so that people can increase their efforts to help the Northeast Volunteer Army. The economic invasion of Japan has created its current brutality, so people should vigorously resist Japanese goods to take their lives. He hopes that the people of the country will work together to save the country by supporting the Volunteer Army and rejecting Japanese goods.

Guest Speeches: Lu Jingshi, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, said in his speech that today is the opening day of the sorrowful variety show, which aims to raise money to support the Northeast Volunteer Army. He hopes that all sectors will be able to donate generously after watching it and fulfill the responsibility of the people in the rear to provide assistance. He also hopes to invite friends and relatives to come here to receive national salvation propaganda. Recently, the retreat of Su Bingwen's troops was due to the lack of support from the rear. Therefore, helping the Volunteer Army is to save China, and saving China is to save ourselves. Lin Kanghou, the representative of the Bankers Association, said that we are holding a variety show while the Northeast Volunteer Army is fighting against a strong enemy in great pain. It can be said that playing the qin under a Coptis chinensis tree is making the best of a bad situation. He hopes that everyone, after seeing the show, can spread the word about the suffering of the refugees and donate one more yuan, which will add one more point of strength to the Volunteer Army. If we can do this, China can be saved. Other speeches were given by variety show committee member Zhang Shichuan and Tao Leqin of the Chinese Taxpayers Association. Due to their length, they are not recorded.

Acknowledgments: Finally, Deputy Executive Director Zhu Xuefan gave a thank-you speech, saying that today's opening ceremony has been supported by all sectors. In addition to extending sincere thanks on behalf of the association, there is one more contribution, that is, today's invitation to all sectors is not for entertainment, but to receive propaganda, and it is hoped that after receiving propaganda, everyone can fully develop the spirit of national salvation and do their best to help the Northeast Volunteer Army.

Today's Program: Today's variety show program is extremely rich. Women's Temperance Union Suggests Saving Beggars 145

The Chinese Women's Temperance Union, in view of the existence of beggars, which violates humanity and humiliates the country, has spared no effort in its work to save beggars for more than a decade. Now that the Municipal Council has been established, the union made a suggestion to the Municipal Council yesterday, asking the Municipal Government to contact the authorities in various concessions to cooperate in carrying out this work. However, as the matter is of great importance, the union earnestly hopes that all groups will rise up to urge the implementation, so that compatriots in this city who are in dire straits can have a place to settle down, setting an example for the whole country. Here is an excerpt from the original text of the suggestion:

For the matter of making a suggestion, every winter, a large number of beggars beg in the streets, which is harmful to humanity, endangers people's livelihoods, disrupts public order, and humiliates the country. In view of this, our union, in addition to establishing the Women and Children's Education and Rehabilitation Center on Xiangyin Road, Jiangwan, to carry out small-scale beggar relief on its own, has repeatedly suggested to the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau to quickly eliminate beggars to enhance the city's appearance and facilitate the people's lives. However, year after year, it has not been implemented. At the beginning of the establishment of your council, our union dares not to presume and earnestly appeals again. If your council can understand public opinion and convey it to the Municipal Government for implementation as soon as possible, the people of the whole city will be grateful without limit. We respectfully present our views as far as we can, briefly stated as follows: "Measures" Please order the responsible subordinates of the Municipal Government (the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus) to quickly contact the Public Concession and the French Concession authorities (as the Chinese area and the concessions are adjacent, if they do not contact each other and cooperate in a unified manner, there will inevitably be the evil of eliminating them here and fleeing there) and various charitable organizations and other important groups in the city to organize a beggar relief committee to plan and implement the work, with special responsibility for implementation. A wise government should first eliminate harm for the people. If beggars can be properly settled, it will not only be the glory of the country's future, but also the desire of the people of the whole city. Whether the above is appropriate is subject to decision. This is addressed to Shi, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, from the Chinese Women's Temperance Union.

New Water Pipe Installation in South Shanghai 147

Based on Water Meter Diameter

Residents in the South Shanghai district who use tap water find that their inlet pipe diameter is often larger than the water meter diameter. For example, a 13mm water meter might be connected to a 20mm inlet pipe. The reason for this is mainly that in the past, the pressure from the inland water company was slightly weaker, and this was intended to compensate. However, this unnecessarily increased labor and material costs. Now that the inland water plant has switched to electric power, the water pressure has increased, and there is no concern about insufficient flow. Moreover, Article 12 of the city's water supply regulations stipulates that the branch pipes in lanes should be installed according to the number of double faucets, based on a 13mm diameter. This means that if a user only installs one pair of faucets and does not plan to add more, a 13mm inlet pipe is sufficient. It is now reported that the responsible department of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has notified all registered water pipe merchants in South Shanghai that in the future, when installing water pipes for users, they should follow the regulations to save costs, unless there is a plan to add more faucets.

Centenarian Li Fangxiao

Suing Fo Ci Pharmaceutical Factory for Damaging Reputation 150

Fo Ci Pharmaceutical Factory arbitrarily uses a centenarian's photo in newspaper advertisements to promote longevity drugs.

The centenarian sues for 10,000 yuan in damages to support the Northeast Volunteer Army.

Li Fangxiao, a 110-year-old man from Zhengzhou, Henan Province, is a Muslim who resides in the Xiaotaoyuan Mosque inside the Old West Gate. Recently, he hired lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Ni Jiong to file a criminal self-accusation against Feng Mingzheng, manager of the Fo Ci Pharmaceutical Factory at No. 35 Renji Road in the British Concession (Hangzhou native), for damaging his reputation in the First Special District Court. He also filed a civil suit seeking 10,000 yuan in damages. The complaint stated: "To prevent damage to reputation, I request legal investigation and a civil suit. I have always valued morality and self-discipline, which is why I have reached such an advanced age. I have never been criticized by anyone in society. However, on October 19th of this year, my portrait appeared in the newspaper, along with my name and age. It was found that Feng Mingzheng (the defendant), the manager of the Fo Ci Pharmaceutical Factory, published it without my consent to use it as a drug advertisement. This clearly violates my personal rights. Among personal rights, freedom rights and name rights are the most important. The factory manager disregarded this and used my portrait and name as an advertisement to sell drugs to deceive the public and satisfy his desire for illegitimate gains. People will suspect that I received illegal benefits from the factory, which is why I allowed them to use my name and photo as a tool for deception. This has greatly damaged my reputation and credibility. I have lived to a great age and have never taken the longevity drugs produced by the factory. Regardless of whether the drug has the effect of prolonging life, the very meaning of the words 'longevity' and 'anti-aging' is illogical, which proves its fraudulence. Moreover, it was published without my consent, which further confirms that the drugs they sell are not what they claim. Those who are deceived will inevitably affect me, which is undoubtedly. Therefore, I specially request your court to take note, order the defendant Feng Mingzheng to appear in court, and punish him for the crime under Article 330 of the Criminal Code. Furthermore, I request that the entire judgment be published in accordance with Article 332 of the same law so that the public is aware. As for the civil suit, I request that the defendant be ordered to compensate me for 10,000 yuan in damages in accordance with Article 19 of the Civil Code, which I will use to support the Northeast Volunteer Army to clarify rewards and punishments and maintain human rights." The court approved the request. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zhen presided over the hearing. The old man, Li Fangxiao, was energetic, with white hair and a youthful face, and a white beard that reached his abdomen. Wearing a leather hat and a blue cloth robe, he stood in the plaintiff's witness box and spoke eloquently, saying that the defendant used his photo for advertising to make money, disregarding his wishes, and made insulting remarks about religion and superstition. The defendant, Feng Mingzheng, testified that he was 26 years old, and the plaintiff's photo was taken by a certain introducer at the Jixing Photo Studio in the French Concession. Because he enjoyed longevity, which is rare these days, it was printed in the newspaper to show that China has such a long-lived old man, so that Chinese and foreigners would respect him, and not to use it for advertising. He said that he had obtained consent before taking the photo. The old man denied this, saying that the defendant's words were false and that he had never been to the Jixing Photo Studio and had never met him. The defendant said that the photo studio had already closed down and the owner had left Shanghai, otherwise, he could be called to testify. He also said that after the newspaper was published, the plaintiff sent a letter scolding him, and he immediately replied to apologize, saying that he respected his age and printed it in the newspaper without any other intention. Judge Wu ordered both parties to withdraw and set a date for further review. This scene of a centenarian arguing with a young man in court is truly unprecedented.

Chinese Tramway Injures Mr. and Mrs. Hua Shousong 152

Recently, the trams of the China Tramway Company have been extremely crowded, and boarding and alighting takes a lot of time, which interferes with the scheduled timetable. Therefore, at each stop, there are often incidents of rushing to ring the bell and start the tram. Yesterday at 3:30 PM, Tram No. 48 on Route 3 of the company was passing the Fangbang Bridge station when Hua Shousong, a 26-year-old clerk from Ying County in the Personnel Section of the First Division of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and his wife, Ma Maihe, 27, were boarding the tram at the station. Because there were still many passengers who had not alighted, they stood by the tram and waited. Unexpectedly, the ticket seller No. 29 immediately rang the bell, and the tram started. The couple was pushed against the tram by the alighting passengers and dragged by the tram. Only after the crowd shouted loudly did the tram stop. Hua's right face was slightly scratched, and Hua's wife's right leg was slightly injured, but the buttons on her cheongsam were torn off. They immediately negotiated with the ticket seller. Subsequently, police officer Zhou Weidong from Post No. 5 of the Second District arrived to mediate. As a result, the tram was allowed to continue, but the clerk Hua Shousong removed the copper badge of ticket seller No. 29 and went to the Second District Headquarters with the police officer to report the incident. The district chief was out, so the district police chief Hu Naitong registered the incident and reported it to the district chief, pending further investigation.

Reader's Advisor 158

Mr. Weng's message: I am thirty-one years old this year and currently working as a principal in an elementary school, with an annual salary of less than three hundred yuan! Besides supporting a wife and two young daughters, I also have to support two elderly mothers and four younger siblings. In recent years, things have not gone well at work, resulting in debts of over three thousand yuan. Now that the end of the year is approaching, those seeking repayment are constantly at my door. I have considered suicide several times to end my life, but I feel uneasy about my young children! In this dilemma, I implore you, sir, to provide me with a complete solution, so that I may find a glimmer of hope. Your merit would be truly immeasurable!

Reply: We deeply sympathize with your meager income and heavy burdens. Moreover, this kind of difficulty is not unique to you; seven or eight out of ten people in the country experience it. We receive numerous letters daily recounting financial difficulties, and this is truly a societal problem that is difficult to alleviate individually. Therefore, your letter asking us for a complete solution... A method isn't without existence, but it would take a long explanation, and the result still wouldn't be able to relieve your "immediate crisis." What we can offer you at present is only the advice to "endure and cope." In our opinion, owing debts is not illegal. Since your debt is not due to your own extravagance, society should be more forgiving. If society isn't forgiving, then just face them with nothing to your name and let society curse you as it pleases. They won't swallow you whole, so what are you afraid of? Are you afraid of not having food in the future? If being a "principal" doesn't work out, the whole family can work. As long as you can endure hardship, you won't starve. If you think that working is shameful, then your thinking is deteriorating, and there's nothing we can do about it. As for your talk of "suicide," that's even more ridiculous. You're alive in this world, so you should ask society for food, why commit suicide?

Mr. Huang Qian's message: I am a twenty-year-old youth who, due to difficult circumstances, only completed junior high school. Three years ago, I was introduced to work through a relative. Now, based on my observations in service, I deeply need advanced knowledge and want to continue my studies in school to avoid lacking opportunities in the future. However, when seeking opinions from relatives and friends, very few express sympathy. For the sake of careful consideration, I cannot help but seek your guidance. My relatives and friends' opinions can be generally summarized as follows: "What's the use of studying? Aren't many college graduates unable to find jobs these days? Isn't it still those with power who can secure a livelihood?" This is what experienced colleagues and elders say. "There are no truly good schools to study in now. It's better to self-study or take supplementary classes in your spare time. You should know that we can learn anywhere; school is just one way to study," a relative said very earnestly to me. They all make very good points. On one hand, I also feel that what is learned in school now doesn't meet the needs of society, and it would be a pity to give up my position, so I'm hesitant! But if I miss this opportunity, I'm afraid I won't have another chance to study, which makes me extremely troubled! Sir, my circumstances are difficult, as mentioned above. The debt my family incurred for my junior high school education has only just been cleared. Now, I only have some savings that can cover two years of schooling. If I go back to school, then I will have to borrow again, and my debt will definitely be even greater! Beloved sir, in my situation, should I continue my studies or take supplementary classes in my spare time? How should we young people strive to learn so that we can achieve success in our careers? Finally, I hope for your sincere advice so that I can quickly decide on a path. I am extremely grateful.

Reply: Your ambition for learning is deeply admirable! Of the two points mentioned in your letter, the latter is very correct. Given your family's difficult economic situation, continuing to study in school would indeed be difficult in reality. It is best to pursue self-study in your spare time. You should know that if a person has true knowledge, their background is completely irrelevant. You don't need to be troubled.

Mr. Lin Danchi's message: At the age of eighteen, I already became a victim of the old feudal marriage system. When discussing marriage, I firmly resisted, but needless to say, that resistance was ineffective. So I had to resign myself to fate, hoping that the heavens would have mercy and grant me a good wife! Heaven knows, she is hopeless. Thus, after living together for less than two nights, our walls of opposition were already firmly built. After the wedding, the second night, I brought up the matter of divorce. This she did not consider a problem, because she had this as her backing: "I didn't come to you for nothing; I was brought back with a grand wedding." Relying on these two phrases, she can wantonly display her inferiorities. What kind of person is she actually? I know that a toad doesn't dare to dream of swan meat, but a woman like her is truly frightening to behold, and I truly can't bear to endure her anymore. She hasn't read any books, has a body full of bad habits, speaks extremely abruptly, and will start a fight at the slightest provocation. As for her appearance, that's beyond discussion. I can only adopt passive means and have distanced myself from her for more than four years. Now, I only want to divorce her, but she consistently disagrees, and my old mother is also unwilling. But when I consider the wishes and interests of those two, my personal happiness and future are completely forfeited, which I absolutely cannot do. What can be done? Here I want to ask: If the other party doesn't agree, can I unilaterally file for divorce with the court or issue a statement in the newspaper to sever relations? Can forced marriages of the past be declared invalid now? Before these questions are resolved, can I have a loving relationship with another woman or discuss marriage? When discussing it, should I clearly tell her about my family situation or keep it a secret for now? If necessary, can I declare a break from family relations as a complete solution?

Reply: The lack of freedom in marriage is indeed a kind of pain felt by the majority of modern youth. If the situation described in your letter is true, then divorce is the right thing to do. However, divorce requires certain legal procedures. A unilateral statement in the newspaper to sever relations is not effective. The best scenario is naturally a divorce by mutual agreement. If one party doesn't agree, then it must be decided by the court. According to Article 1052 of the current Civil Code, divorce must meet certain conditions. Therefore, from a legal perspective, divorce at present cannot be said to be absolutely free. Regarding this point, you must consider this yourself when suing the court. Also, before the marital relationship is severed, you cannot marry another person, otherwise, it constitutes bigamy, which must not be attempted.

Important News 162

The Ministry of Education proposes to the National Congress that no new middle schools should be established within two years. The Ministry of Education plans to propose to the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee that no new public or private general middle schools should be established within two years, and that efforts should be made to improve and enrich the existing public and private middle schools in terms of quality. The detailed proposal is currently being drafted and should be submitted to the General Assembly for review in the coming days.

On the 17th, the Ministry of Education sent Chen Kezhong, a full-time editor of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, to Fujian to inspect public and private secondary schools and universities above the secondary level, as well as Xiamen University. Chen left Beijing for Shanghai on the 17th and will transfer to a ship to Fujian.

Teachers and Staff of Middle Schools in Jiangsu Province Continue to Petition 165

Submitting Opinions to the Ministry of Education on Methods of Service for Teachers and Staff

Requesting that the Education Funding Management Office issue at least one month's cash advance

More than 30 representatives from various schools attending the Interim Plenary Representatives Conference of the Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Teachers and Staff (Zhang Shaonan from Huaiyin arrived today) gathered at the Second Hospital of Nanzhong on the morning of the 17th to discuss funding matters. Although the Management Office has agreed to issue notices in installments, this is a long-term solution that cannot meet immediate needs. Therefore, at a minimum, they must receive cash advances for the second half of August and the first half of September before they can leave Beijing and return to their respective schools. The representatives from seven schools, including Nanzhong, Suzhou Middle School, Zhenjiang Normal School, Yangzhou Middle School, Shanghai Middle School, Wuxi Middle School, and Wujiang Rural Normal School, who were sent to the Ministry of Education to petition yesterday, returned to the meeting place at noon to report. When they went to the Ministry of Education in the morning, they were received by Gu Shusen, Director of the General Education Department. The representatives stated that the "Methods of Service and Treatment for Teachers and Staff of Secondary Schools" promulgated by the Ministry of Education did not conform to actual conditions and expressed their opinions in accordance with the resolutions: 1. Implement a full-time system and not calculate salaries based on teaching hours. 2. The number of teaching hours per week is too high and should be reduced. 3. Salaries should be increased. 4. The median of teaching hours should be used to calculate the median of salaries. 5. Those who take on class training duties should have their teaching hours reduced. 6. Eliminate the difficulty of elective courses. 7. The Legislative Yuan passed the "Organizational Law of Normal Schools," but there is no status for rural normal schools, and remedial measures should be requested. Director Gu replied: 1. Regarding the curriculum standards, the Ministry has decided to implement them for new students admitted in the fall of next year. The existing grades will follow the old standards (i.e., those who have already taken electives will continue until graduation, without changes midway). The reason for abolishing the elective system is that independent vocational schools of various types, including normal schools, have already been established. General middle schools are for the purpose of further education, so it is not appropriate to have electives. Compulsory subjects should be studied. 2. Regarding the issue of rural normal schools, there are currently 559 rural normal schools nationwide. Since difficulties have arisen in practice, the Ministry of Education has already submitted a proposal to the Central Political Council requesting that a way be found to supplement the policy. In the future, rural normal schools may be added to the Organizational Law of Normal Schools. 3. Regarding the issues of service and treatment, such as teaching hours, the Ministry of Education originally drafted the standards to be similar to those set by provincial schools. During the meeting, the standards were revised by various committee members with reference to the teaching hours of teachers in Western countries. Now that difficulties are being felt, fortunately, there is room for flexibility in the instructions of the methods promulgated by the Ministry. The public generally agreed that the Executive Committee should submit a document to the Department of Education requesting that the Ministry of Education make appropriate changes to the previously promulgated methods based on actual circumstances. The meeting adjourned in the afternoon. At 7 PM in the evening, all the representatives went to the Education Funding Management Office, where they were received by Director Niu. Director Niu reported that Section Chief Yang had not returned, and he had written a letter to Chairman Gu of the Jiangsu Provincial Government yesterday evening to earnestly entrust him to work with the Finance Department to come up with a solution. Therefore, the current fund-raising is being carried out in three ways: 1. Demanding outstanding payments from the Provincial Government. 2. Urging various departments to lend money. 3. Borrowing money from banks. By gathering funds from these three sources, it should be possible to achieve the desired outcome. Wu Dezhang reported that the representatives had decided that the minimum requirement was one month's cash advance. Liu Beihe reported that the notice for the second half of August could be filled out the day after tomorrow and the funds could be withdrawn on the 25th of this month. The notice for September must wait until the audit meeting on the 25th to be signed. The due date for withdrawal is between the 10th and 15th of January. The notice for October will also be signed at the audit meeting on December 25th. The due date for withdrawal is between the 15th and 25th of January. The notice for November can be allocated to the counties for collection. After exchanging opinions, the situation will be reported in detail tomorrow.

Special Feature

Speaking Out for Middle Schools Nationwide (4) Liao Maoru 170

(4) Changing Things in the Middle of the Academic Year Only Creates Confusion

This is a matter of fact. The allocation of teachers' time, the arrangement of timetables, and the selection of courses must all go through a considerable period of preparation, usually before the start of the first semester, to prepare for the work of the entire academic year. At the start of the second semester, only minor changes can be made. Now, completely overturning the old regulations and with nothing to base things on, each school must re-establish new regulations, stipulate transitional measures, dismiss some old teachers, hire new teachers, establish new timetables, and select new textbooks. All these things cannot be done immediately. The losses to the school and the losses to the students during this period are unknown. Anyone with some experience in school administration knows this situation and need not elaborate.

(5) The Number of Service Hours Stipulated for Middle School Teachers and Staff is Too Ideal. According to the new methods promulgated by the Ministry of Education, full-time teachers in secondary schools, in addition to bearing responsibility for moral education and extracurricular self-study guidance, must teach 22 to 26 hours per week in junior high school and 20 to 24 hours per week in senior high school. In special circumstances, this must be increased appropriately. The teaching time for staff members who teach is based on the teaching time of full-time teachers. At a minimum, the principal must teach no less than one-half, and the head of academic affairs and the head of moral education must teach no less than two-thirds. Experience tells us that this standard is untenable. In American middle schools, teachers teach an average of 21 to 22 hours a week. In Japanese middle schools, teachers teach an average of 19 hours. According to our country's experience, it is most appropriate for responsible original teachers (of course, the Ministry of Education hopes that every teacher is responsible) to teach 18 to 20 hours per week. If teachers participate in some extracurricular work in addition to these many hours, they are already busy enough. If they must take on moral education duties and self-study guidance, their hours must be reduced by two or three hours per week. We know that for every hour of teaching, the preparation before class and the handling after class must take at least one or two hours (if the time is shorter, the book will definitely not be taught well). Therefore, teaching 20 hours of class, plus the time spent on extracurricular activities, plus the time spent on preparation and handling, already requires more than 50 hours. If we follow the regulations of the Ministry of Education, each teacher must work more than 80 hours a week, otherwise, they can only buy books in the classroom, and they cannot pay attention to any preparation, practice, looking at notes, correcting compositions, grading exam papers, etc. According to our experience, principals, heads of academic affairs, and heads of moral education can teach at most 8 or 9 hours of lessons per week. Any more will hinder their duties.

I remember Russell saying in his book "Education and the Modern World," "A young person has a desire for knowledge. The disappearance of this desire is mostly because the knowledge given to them exceeds their needs and capacity, just as children all like food, but once they are forced, they develop an unwelcome attitude." We hope that the curriculum promulgated by the Ministry of Education will take into account the abilities of young people and their interests, and not provide them with knowledge that they cannot accept, and not force them to learn lessons that they do not particularly like. "Children must first be treated as children, and only then as students." Knowledge is certainly important, but other aspects may be equally important. We further hope that the Ministry of Education will take into account the abilities and interests of teachers and staff. Education is a spiritual undertaking. To improve the spirit of teachers and staff, we must use effective methods, and we cannot forcibly increase their workload. Chinese education is like an unopened flower, which has suffered the ravages of wind and rain, exposing a state of hardship. We only hope that the Ministry of Education will be a protector of flowers, paying attention to cultivation and no longer doing things that stifle growth. That dying flower may be able to see the sun again, donate fragrance, and absorb the air of freedom. (End)

Curriculum Standards for Junior High Schools (9)

Chemistry I, Objectives 171

1. To clarify the mutual relationships in ordinary things and natural phenomena and to have common scientific knowledge;

2. To know the relationship between nature and life and the methods of utilizing nature;

3. To cultivate good habits of paying attention to natural phenomena and things anytime and anywhere;

4. To train the ability of observation, investigation, and thinking;

5. To be edified by science and be able to comprehend that diligence, honesty, agility, organization, and other virtues are the foundation for successful careers.

II. Time Allocation

Please study for one academic year, four hours per semester, and another semester for three hours, totaling seven hours.

III. Syllabus Outline

1. Air ㈠ Relationship between respiration and combustion and air; ㈡ Ratio of components (oxygen, nitrogen); ㈢ Metal oxides.

2. Water ㈠ Natural water; ㈡ Distilled water; ㈢ Composition of water; ㈣ Hydrogen.

3. Salt ㈠ Source and composition; ㈡ Hydrochloric acid; ㈢ Chlorine gas and bleaching powder.

4. Sulfur ㈠ Sulfur oxide; ㈡ Sulfuric acid; ㈢ Sulfide minerals and sulfates.

5. Nitric acid and nitrates (saltpeter, Chile saltpeter, etc.).

6. Helium: source, properties, and uses.

7. Carbon ㈠ Allotropes of carbon (charcoal, coal, graphite, diamond); ㈡ Formation and types of coal, dry distillation of coal, coal gas and petroleum; ㈢ Carbon dioxide; ㈣ Main carbonates and natural carbonates (calcite, chalk, limestone, stalactites, stalagmites, etc.), alkali (sodium carbonate), source, properties, and uses.

8. Phosphorus ㈠ Phosphorus and matches; ㈡ Phosphoric acid and phosphates (apatite, superphosphate fertilizer).

9. Arsenic

10. Silicon dioxide and silicates.

11. Glass

12. Borax and boric acid.

13. Iron ㈠ Types and properties of iron; ㈡ Main iron ores; ㈢ Uses of iron.

14. Precious metals ㈠ Gold; ㈡ Silver and currency, decorative alloys; ㈢ Tin.

15. Common metals ㈠ Alkali metals, sodium, and sodium hydroxide, Beryllium and its alloys; ㈡ Alkaline earth metals lime; ㈢ Magnesium group metals, A Zinc and galvanized iron, B Mercury; ㈣ Aluminum, alum, feldspar, mica, clay, ceramics; ㈤ Tin group metals, A Tin and tinplate, B Lead and dyes, C Antimony and type metal, D Bismuth and its uses.

16. Wine and alcohol.

17. Nutrients ㈠ Standards of food composition; ㈡ Sugar and starch; ㈢ Fats and oils, soap; ㈣ Protein, tofu and milk.

18. Cotton, paper, wool, silk, rayon.

19. Main terminology: Mixture, compound, component, element, atom, molecule, physical change, solution, evaporation, solidification, deliquescence, filtration, precipitation, distillation, crystallization, chemical change, combination, electrolysis, fermentation, reaction (law of conservation of mass), oxidation, reduction, analysis, synthesis, chemical symbol, molecular formula, chemical equation, dissolution, solubility, saturation, acid, base, alkali salt, acidic reaction, alkaline reaction, neutralization. Note: Teaching materials should pay attention to domestic products. Special attention should be paid to national defense chemistry.

IV. Summary of Implementation Methods

Teaching Points

Start with things commonly encountered in daily life or phenomena shown by experiments, first making students have a strong interest in the problem, and then slowly introducing the teaching materials. The sequence is nothing more than: ㈠ Presenting one or two phenomena observed daily or the results obtained from classroom demonstrations; ㈡ Asking questions; ㈢ Introducing the teaching materials; ㈣ Often, within the possible range, asking students if there are other daily problems that can be solved with the teaching materials of this section. For example:

Air

㈠ What are the consequences of choking an animal's trachea or mouth and nose? If kerosene is carelessly used, what method should be used to extinguish it? Introduce the relationship between air and respiration and combustion. ㈡ Place a small amount of red phosphorus on a cork floating on the water surface and ignite it with fire. Cover it with a 250 cubic centimeter wide-mouth bottle. Ask students to pay attention to the following points: A. Is there any red phosphorus left? B. Is there any air left? C. How much of the remaining part is there? Even though the bottle is simple, there is still air in it. Why doesn't the red phosphorus continue to burn? From this, introduce the composition of air and the ratio of oxygen and nitrogen in the air, and the properties and uses of oxygen. ㈢ Why does iron rust? What are the methods to prevent rusting? From this, introduce metal oxides. Note: Regarding products, attention should be paid to domestic materials.

First World Esperanto Exhibition 173

Esperanto was created by Zamenhof of Poland, aiming to be an international language for the unification of languages ​​of all countries in the world. It has a history of 45 years. Since the Chinese Esperanto Association organized and promoted it, more than 2,000 Chinese people have learned it, and there is an Esperanto bookstore and correspondence school to promote it. The association held a World Esperanto Exhibition at the New World Hotel on Tibet Road the day before yesterday, displaying more than 2,000 kinds of Esperanto books, more than 300 kinds of magazines, and dozens of kinds of books and photos. Three to four hundred people visited each day, and Esperanto booklets and the first issue of the journal were distributed.

Yesterday, due to the school's sixth anniversary, a celebration ceremony was held in the morning, with more than 400 students and guests attending. The founders Yu Jifan and Pan Boying reported, and Principal Xu Langxi, Dean Wang Yachen, and Professor Hua Lin gave speeches. At 2:00 PM, a tea party was held, and there were gifts. Every teacher and student of the school was given a gift or a self-made artwork, which could be exchanged for a gift. At the same time, ancient paintings and works by the school's professors were exhibited, with deep and interesting flavors, and it was a very grand occasion.

Jiangnan University Football Match: Referee Chen Jixiang Beaten; Fudan and Jiaotong Universities Draw 0-0 186

Fudan Students Assault Referee

The Jiangnan University Athletic Association's football matches have historically been rife with disputes, including players fighting each other or referees being beaten. The match between Zhong Gong and Guanghua a few years ago even resulted in bloodshed and litigation, which is not a good sign for university football. Yesterday, Fudan and Jiaotong Universities competed at Jiangwan. The two sides were evenly matched and neither achieved a breakthrough. The referee, Chen Jixiang, is astute and capable, and one of the best Chinese football referees in Shanghai. Aware of the difficulty of refereeing Jiangnan University football matches, he was particularly careful yesterday, observing everything meticulously and impartially. Therefore, the competition between the two teams was very peaceful, and the result was a draw, which should not have led to any unfortunate events. Unexpectedly, after the match ended, a small number of Fudan students expressed their dissatisfaction with the referee. They shouted for an attack and surrounded Chen Jixiang. Foreign-style wooden instruments flew through the air. The captain of the Fudan cheerleading squad, wearing a baseball catcher's chest protector and mask, struck Chen on the head with a baseball bat. His scalp was cut open, and blood flowed profusely, staining his shirt collar. Order was immediately disrupted, and Jiangnan University football suffered another bloody incident.

Equal Strength Between the Two Teams: Jinan, Jiaotong, and Fudan Universities are the Most Hopeful Contenders for the Jiangnan University Title This Year. Yesterday, Fudan and Jiaotong Universities competed at Jiangwan Fudan University. Because of the importance of the match, Chen Jixiang, a famous football referee from the Chinese Athletic Referees Association, was specially invited to officiate. Students from both universities enthusiastically cheered their teams. Although Jiaotong University had a long journey, more than a hundred supporters accompanied the team. The two teams were evenly matched, with balanced attacks. The forwards and defenders all performed well, but they lacked scoring talent, resulting in no goals. However, the performance was quite satisfactory. A Glimpse of the Competition: The match started at 2:30 PM. The two sides had equal attacks and were evenly matched. Near the end of the first half, Jiaotong University had a strong momentum and repeatedly tried to penetrate Fudan's goal, but Fudan's defense was tight, and there was no opportunity. At the beginning of the second half, Fudan was full of energy and aggressive, launching repeated attacks. However, Yu Xuzhang repeatedly missed opportunities, much to his frustration. Later, Jiaotong University counterattacked Fudan, but was also unsuccessful. With only ten minutes left, both sides were determined to win, and the situation suddenly became tense. Wan Xianghua of Jiaotong University attempted a side attack on Fudan's goal but missed. Fudan then advanced. Long Yixun shot the ball within Jiaotong University's penalty area, hitting a Jiaotong University defender on the shoulder. Fudan students shouted, "Jiaotong University committed a handball!" The situation became chaotic, and shouts filled the air. Some people even attempted to attack the referee, but they were stopped by Fudan instructor Chen Bingde and the players. The match continued, and the result was a draw. The Behavior of University Students: The match ended in a draw, and it was thought that everything would be peaceful. Unexpectedly, Fudan students were unwilling to accept the result and protested against the referee Chen Jixiang. Shouts arose from all around, and they rushed onto the field, surrounding Chen. They temporarily used trumpets, flagpoles, and other items as weapons, throwing them around in the air, causing great chaos. The captain of the cheerleading squad, wearing a baseball catcher's chest protector and mask, charged into the crowd, wielding a baseball bat as if facing a formidable enemy, and struck Chen on the head, breaking his scalp and causing profuse bleeding. Chen was then protected by Fudan players and taken to the gymnasium office. Such behavior by university students is regrettable. The lineups of the two teams yesterday were as follows:
